[30;1m10 | [0m[35m# Solders[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m12 | [0m[35m`solders` is a high-performance Python toolkit for Solana, written in Rust. It provides robust solut[0m
[30;1m13 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m14 | [0m[35m- Core SDK stuff: keypairs, pubkeys, signing and serializing transactions - that sort of thing.[0m
[30;1m15 | [0m[35m- RPC stuff: building requests and parsing responses (no networking stuff - if you want help with th[0m
[30;1m16 | [0m[35m[solana-py](https://michaelhly.github.io/solana-py/rpc/async_api/) is your friend).[0m
